## Diagram 4

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[Start test_container_to_trip_write] --> B[Create CrudOperations instance]
    B --> C[Create containerToTripLeg1 using from_dict]
    C --> D[Log containerToTripLeg1]
    D --> E[Create containerToTripLeg2 using set methods]
    E --> F[Create containerToTripLeg3 using direct assignment]
    F --> G[Create row for containerToTripLeg1]
    G --> H[Create row for containerToTripLeg2]
    H --> I[Create row for containerToTripLeg3]
    I --> J[Store test_uuid]
    J --> K[Assert containerToTripLeg1.id is string]
    K --> L[Assert containerToTripLeg2.id is string]
    L --> M[Assert containerToTripLeg3.id is string]
    M --> N[End test]
```
